    WHERE ([i3].[IsAttending] = 1) AND ([wedding].[Id] = [i3].[WeddingId])
) AS [AttendingGuests], [wedding].[Id]
FROM [Weddings] AS [wedding]
INNER JOIN [Agencies] AS [wedding.Agency] ON [wedding].[AgencyId] = [wedding.Agency].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [People] AS [wedding.Bridegroom] ON [wedding].[BridegroomId] = [wedding.Bridegroom].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [People] AS [wedding.Bride] ON [wedding].[BrideId] = [wedding.Bride].[Id]
ORDER BY (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Invitations] AS [i]
    WHERE [wedding].[Id] = [i].[WeddingId]
) DESC, (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Invitations] AS [i0]
    WHERE ([i0].[IsAttending] = 1) AND ([wedding].[Id] = [i0].[WeddingId])
)" (0723d8ff)
